<Author>arianneleigh
<Content>Good hotel The hotel was a very nice stop on my way through Italy. I booked on the hotel website. When I arrived via train the directions supplied by the hotel made my walk from the station simple. The single flight of stairs from the street to the first floor were a bit daunting but the man from the desk carried my suitcase up (I had to carry it down myself when I checked out). The rooms were clean and modern with private bathrooms. As I was travelling alone my single room was on the small side but I was only paying 49 euros a night so I was happy with it. The location was good. Market mere steps from the hotel. Restaurants close by. Easy walk to the Duomo and the David.

<Author>mum39
<Content>Great Hotel in Florence We are a 60+ couple, just back from a super Short Break in Florence at The Hotel Globus.The location was perfect, within easy walking distance from Train and Bus Stations, and in a street with lots of character, good inexpensive places to eat (including the cafes at the Market, just a few strides away) and also easy walking to the wonderful sights in this amazing city.The stairs up to Reception weren't really a problem, as we travelled light with just a bag each.However, at the end of our stay, the heavy bag was carried down for us.All the staff we met were really friendly and helpful, and we were able to help ourselves to tea or coffee as we chatted to them.The cleanliness of the Hotel was excellent, with clean towels each day, and we rather liked the heavy curtains, keeping the room dark for a comfortable sleep in the early morning.The double windows seemed fairly successful, but we did get some street noise on our last night.. We enjoyed the breakfasts, a good variety of fresh food, and no queues for the dining room in October!The Internet access was a bonus, and the lift good for going back to our room after long days of sight-seeing. We can also recommend the excellent bus service, and the charming young lady in the Tourist Office by Santa Maria Novellawho advised us about the Tickets.We would certainly stay at Hotel Globus again, and have no hesitation in adding our recommendation to the many others on this website.

<Author>EdandJill
<Content>Loved the Florence Globus We stayed at the Globus Hotel in Florence for 10 days in September,2008 and found it to be a fabulous choice. first of all , it is well situated, close to the Santa Maria Novella train station and the Sita bus station.It is also within walking distance to the San Lorenzo indoor and outdoor markets,and other major attractions in Florence(such as the Duomo,Uffizi Gallery, Academia,Ponte Vecchio). we intially booked an economy room but asked for an upgrade,mainly because we were staying for 10 days. The owners obliged us and put us into a superior room, which included free laptop/internet and free minibar. The view from our bedroom window looked out to the Medici Church in the San Loenzo Piazza. The room was always very clean and well appointed in a modern style of furnishings.The Owners (Serena and Michele)and ALL STAFF were friendly and very helpful.We asked a lot of questions about tours,scooters, computers and all questions were answered with enthusiasm.THe breakfasts were always well balanced and included juice,tea,(good quality choices), special coffees from a very nice fellow, dry cereals,fresh and dried fruit, ham, cheese, tomatoes, white and wholewheat bread, white and wholewheat buns and croissants and yogurt.The breakfast room and lobby both have CNN in English,(the rooms also have SKY cable)The lobby is on the 2nd. floor,there is an elevator to the other floors.Our stay will be forever in our memories and will recommend the Globus to our friends. WE rate this hotel 5 out of 5.

<Author>ClaireLouEngland
<Content>Great Location and Friendly Staff We stayed at the Hotel Globus during a 3 week trip around Italy and were happy with choice of hotel due to its location, within walking distance of all the main sites, and the friendly and helpful staff. The area is quite lively with plenty of restaurants and shops. We did find it a little noisy in the morning as the market runs along the same street as the hotel but it wasn't a major problem. If, like us, you arrive late in the evening don鈥檛 be put off by the rubbish on the streets, this is due to the market being packed up for the evening and the streets are back to normal in the morning. The staff at the hotel Globus are extremely welcoming, especially the staff on reception and the gentleman that serves breakfast. Don't let the entrance to the hotel deter you, once you are upstairs the hotel is very modern and clean. The room itself was very compact, same width as a double bed with tiny bathroom but we expected this from the description and didn鈥檛 spend much time in there except to sleep. We loved the mini lift and free internet access in the lobby. The only problem was the air conditioning unit which seemed to work on a timer and you couldn't set it to your own preferences which meant the room did get quite hot especially when getting ready.If visiting Florence again, which I hope I do as it鈥檚 a truly beautiful city, I would consider the Hotel Globus due to its great location but would upgrade to a larger room. It鈥檚 a great place for people on a city break who would spend most of the day out of the hotel sightseeing and are looking for somewhere clean, convenient and welcoming to sleep after a busy day.

<Author>marshallo
<Content>Highly recommended - go for a "superior" room though We stayed at the Globus for 3 nights - arrived at S.M.N. and eventually figured out that the road it was on WAS actually this small, narrow lane....!As everyone else has said, reception is on the first floor accessed only by stairs - not ideal, but if you're able bodied, not the greatest challenge in the world.Bright, friendly helpful staff - reception, cleaners, the breakfast guy - and clean  tidy communal areas.We'd booked a superior room via the hotel's website - it worked out about 10 euro more than a standard room per night - the difference was worth it. We had rm 309 - on the back - no view to speak of, but laptop with free wifi, comp. non alcoholic drinks from minibar  plenty of space to move about. Bathroom was good as well.Location is great - small gelateria right outside the door, small corner shops (UK phrase!) nearby - the market is at the bottom of the road, and Duomo maybe 10 mins walk away.Make sure you check out the restaurants behind the market (ZaZa's particularly) - at first, it doesn't seem the greatest location to sit out  eat, but good food  atmosphereAll in all, high highly recommended if you're taking a short break in Florence

<Author>Daisy1974
<Content>Excellent hotel - good location We stayed at Hotel Globus for 3 nights in early May. The location was excellent - close to the bus station, which was handy on arrival and within easy walking distance of all the major sights.We stayed in a normal double room, which was nice and clean, though slightly on the smaller side, but we did expect that having read previous reviews and the description on the hotels website. After a bit of research we booked directly with the hotel via their website as this was the cheapest rate. The rate included breakfast , which was a nice buffet with plenty of choice. The hotel also offered free internet service and complimentary tea and coffee all day. However, beware of booking museum tickets through the hotel. We did and it turned out that it would have been cheaper pre-booking directly with the museum. Also if you book through the hotel you cannot choose what time you want to go and they booked us a 9am on a Saturday morning!! Not what we wanted on a relaxing weekend break.Apart from that we could not fault the hotel, a comfortable stay and and good value for money - would stay there again.

<Content>Room with a bit of a view Super little hotel close to the train station - but longer if you can't follow the map on the hotel website! clean modern rooms, great bonus is the free wifi and also the laptops in the rooms.Photo's make hotel common areas look more spacious than they are but rooms are a perfect pit stop for a few days in florence.Breakfast was adequate, usual fair, nothing to write home about, breakfast room was small so could be a bit of a problem when hotel busier. <Author>tripaddicted
<Content>A Gem of Florence We booked a reservation at the Hotel Globus through its web-site based of the good reviews that we read on tripadvisor. Though, we are fully aware that european hotels are less in quality compared with the ones in Asia or US. This is true, therefore we are not expecting much on it.During the time to confirm our reservation, we have been offered with various rate for double standard or double executive room. Thank you to Michelle who is one of the owner of this hotel. He gave us a good deal of Euro 90 for double executive room (incl. buffet breakfast and taxes). We stayed there for 3 nights late December 2003.To us the hotel is most likely a 2 stars with a 4 stars bathroom facility. Our room is spacious with internet access, cozy modern-minimalis design and clean. The one which decreased the value of this hotel is that the lobby is up a flight of stairs. Guests must climb with luggage. when we arrived we were greeted by the front staff who helped us to bring our luggages up to the lobby.We left our luggages at the front desk since the room reserved for us was still occupied. When we came back in the afternoon, our luggages had been brought in the room at 2nd floor. The bar and breakfast place looked like a snack vendor and the only staff is very practical. Breakfast was fine european standard with fresh fruit, however we could ask for a cup of capucinno or even a glass of hot chocolate.This hotel is recommended for budget travelers who do not mind to carry on your own luggages to the room and during check out. We do not mind it either. The location is best, near the train station (5 minutes walk) and many budget eating houses nearby. Mercato St. Lorenzo is just steps from the hotel. The window of our room is facing the back of Medici Chapel, a warm scene in the morning of winter season.We will absolutely stay there again if we get back to Florence one day.xxx

<Author>snarkyarchy
<Content>Stairway to Heaven-Florence's best hotel We arrived in Florence via Eurostar and were a bit freaked out by some of the shady characters lurking around the train station, but our fears were relieved when we were warmly greeted at the Globus Hotel by Nick.The hotel is only a five minute walk from the train station, but far enough away from the Santa Maria Novella area that we felt very safe. The hotel may not be in the heart of Florence, but since most of the attractions are within a ten minute walk of each other, Globus' location is great. At the end of the block, you're right at the Central Market and all the street stalls that set up daily around San Lorenzo. The Duomo is about two blocks away and the Uffizi/Piazza della Signoria is another ten minute walk from the Duomo. The staff was by far the friendliest and most helpful we met on our trip throughout Europe. The breakfast staff was great at making our morning coffees (and you must try their thick and yummy hot chocolate made to order) and the front desk staff was always smiling and ready to chat up the weather and things to do around the city. They even alerted us early on about a scheduled water line shut off planned for the neighborhood due to construction work in the adjoining street. (Although this made us a bit paranoid not to drink anything for a few hours, we were fortunate to be leaving that day and in fact, the water was not turned off to my relief when I had to use the bathroom before our departure.)Since we were traveling with three people, we had a very spacious room done in a minimalist style of dark wood wardrobes, desk and side tables, padded headboards, and tiled floors. Although the room could have used more lighting, it was adequate enough to read by and there was enough light coming in through the windows during day. We had one room with two double beds and an adjoining room with another double bed and a single bathroom. The bathroom had a tub and the much-love heated towel bar. Our favorite feature of the hotel was the Sky TV channels. There was a good variety of shows that could be switched between Italian and English, which was a welcome option to having to only watch CNN International or BBC World. One can take only so much of cheeky international correspondents and anchors.The one thing that we wished we knew about was that there was no lift. Luckily we were on the first floor and only had to walk up one flight of stairs with our luggage (which was nothing compared to the three bridges we had to cross in Venice.) To the credit of the amazing staff, they helped us carry our luggage down when we checked out and wouldn't accept any tips. It was a very gentlemanly thing to do.There was even free internet access in the lobby from noon to 11:30 pm daily. They will give you a login and password to use and it comes in handy if you have to make museum reservations or check changes in flight itineraries.

<Author>dokelly
<Content>Probably the worst hotel I have ever stayed in We stayed here for three nights on a tour of Italy and the hotel was, by far, the worst we stayed in and the worst hotel experience I have ever had. Firstly, the hotel is located in a pretty seedy area and there was the smell of drains outside the front entrance. Superficially, the hotel looks OK, something which is emphasised on the website. However, once you look a bit closer it is quite rough around the edges and generally unclean. We made the mistake of booking an economy room, which was not only tiny but also quite dirty with layers of dust, mould in the bathroom and stained sheets. It was clear that it had not been cleaned properly for some time. However, by far the worst element of the stay was the discovery of bedbugs in our room on the first night. We noticed insects crawling on the walls and black stains as soon as we got to the room and, although at the time we didn't know what they were, we demanded to be moved. We were told there were no spare rooms, we were moved to a ground floor room which was in the process of being built (the bathroom was only half finished) and we were given sheets and forced to make our own beds. The next day, to their credit, the management apologised and refunded the fee for the first night.For the second and third nights we were placed in the adjoining room to the bedbug infested room, which thankfully had no bedbugs. However, we saw that the hotel had put new guests in the infested room. It was only when we returned home armed with photos of the room that I discovered that the 'insects' were in fact bedbugs, and it shocked me that new guests had been put in the room after we refused to stay there. I emailed the hotel, who replied to admit they knew that there were bedbugs in the room but that the problem had since been treated. However, it was obvious from looking back at the photos that the bedbugs had been there for some time and had either been ignored or inexplicably overlooked.All in all, it was just a horrible and worrying experience (bedbugs can travel on suitcases and invest your own home) and I wish the management of the hotel had been straight with us from the start. It was only through a bit of research of my own that I discovered what the creepy crawlies were that we had almost spent a night with. It was appalling that such obvious signs of infestation, which had clearly been there for some time, had not been picked up. Looking at other people's comments, it seems that the standard and superior rooms are perhaps a bit more acceptable which probably explains the mixed reviews. However, I would steer any possible guests away from this hotel given the mediocre condition of the hotel, general uncleanliness, poor location and the general cavalier attitude of the management, that is assuming that the bedbug issues have been resolved.

<Author>mimiccr
<Content>"Economy" rooms VERY small We stayed 3 nights the end of March, 2008, and sorry to be writing my review so late. I can't fault the Globus Hotel for this because I booked the economy room to save a few bucks. It was absolutely tiny, hardly room to walk around the bed. We did manage for the 3 nights because we were out and about every day and evening, but even worse was the noise from the street. We did not have AC because it was in March, but the room would get terribly stuffy in the middle of the night since it was so small, but when we opened the windows, we were right in the front of the hotel on the street and the noise was unbearable.  Now on the bright side: Nick was great and he recommended a wonderful restaurant down the street that was so good, we ate there all three nights. It was had fabulous grilled meats at a very reasonable price. The breakfasts were very good and the coffee was great. The hotel was in a great location for the train station, and I certainly enjoyed the market across the street. I just wanted to warn everyone to stay away from the economy rooms unless you are perhaps one person and really watching your $$. I wish I had spent a little more and gotten a standard or superior room, but they were booked and there was no possibility of an upgrade. We love Florence and I would stay there again, but in a larger room.

<Author>david03
<Content>Hotel Globus Just returned from a long weekend in Florence and stayed at the Hotel Globus.9 in our party in total and we had double, triiple and quadruple rooms, including for 4 children.Although the Hotel is on a narrow side street and probably not the best part of town, this is easily outweighed by its proximity to The Duomo (only a few minutes walk) and all the other city sights. It is almost immediately adjacent to the street and food market.Also, only 5 minutes walk from the rail station so no taxi required - it is better and cheaper to use the train to and from the airport rather than the coach.The rooms are very modern and clean although not much of a view from two of them. However, very quiet at night.The small breakfast/dining area could get crowded and you may well have to wait a few minutes at peak times but well worth it.Nick at the reception is extremely helpful and is a mine of information. He booked our Uffizi tickets in advance (a must!).Spare some time for Pisa. It's quite picturesque. Lots of up-market shops and photos outside the leaning Tower are a must. Although 15 Euros to get in is a bit pricey.We got a through ticket from Firenze Station to the airport (you have to change at Pisa Central Station) but you're allowed a 6 hour stop-off. Leave your buggage at the left luggage office in the Station (3 Euros per item) and do the 20 minute walk to the Tower via the main shopping street.We stayed 3 days and 2 nights and probably needed an extra day to see all the sites. Beware that the museums are closed all day Monday.

<Author>louiseUS
<Content>You get what you pay for! If you are trying to save money, it is fine to stay here but you do get what you pay for. I don't believe that this hotel should qualify as a 3 star hotel any longer. I stayed here 3 years ago, and it did then. However, in the past 3 years it seems to have become worn and a bit run down. The young man at the front desk is very nice which helped. My husband, daughter  myself were staying there (triple room) for 2 nights. First a man (apprx mid to late 20s) tried to rob my husband as my husband walked behind me on the rather narrow street near the hotel minutes prior to checking in. (It is close to the train station.) Fortunately, my husband put him into a fast headlock and pinned him to a car until storeowners came outside. Then (even though reservations were made months in advance) we were assigned to a room on the first floor that smelled badly. (I had told them in advance that I had asthma, and the hotel staff didn't even seem to notice the strong odor in the room.) After begging  pleading, I was told that we could take the quad room next door but would have to move back into the original room for the 2nd night since he said they were booked solid and a quad was coming. The quad room was fine (for the money). It didn't smell but spreads were worn (even a small tear in one) and the shower curtain (thin plastic) was moldy at the bottom. The next morning after begging, pleading etc they said to pack up all of our things and move them out of the quad room before touring and they'd see what they could do about a different room if we came back at noon. They did give us a room on an upper floor. It also smelled however and had worn spreads. There was a bit of mold on the shower curtain but not as bad as the quad room mold. Due to asthma, I also need my head elevated at night and require 2 pillows. The hotel said that they can only provide one pillow per person when they are booked solid because they do not have an extra pillow! My husband had to sleep without a pillow! This hotel was always very basic,utilitarian looking but it didn't appear worn down and faded 3 years ago. I was disappointed and wouldn't choose to stay here again. However, if I were on a strict budget and smells etc didn't bother me, I would consider staying here for the price. The breakfast is fine, the man who makes it is nice and they have free internet. It's a shame though that the hotel doesn't charge $5 extra and allot about $10 per night into a fund and segregate the money and use it to keep their rooms nice by replacing spreads and shower curtains on a regular basis and doing maintenance to prevent odors and problems. Despite someone attempting to rob us, I didn't really feel unsafe even though the hotel is in a rather narrow street.

<Author>enjoythescenery
<Content>LOVED the Globus I'm having a hard time understanding the bad reviews- my boyfriend and I stayed here for 3 days over New Years, and it was an absolutely wonderful choice. My only complaint would be that you have to walk up a flight of stairs to get to the lobby- but anyone reading this site would know that before they book. Also, the staff heard us come in with our luggage and rushed down to help us carry everything up. They also helped when we left.We booked a double superior room- I believe it was Room # 201, and it was wonderful. It was not tiny- I would describe it as cozy. European hotel rooms are not huge, so we didn't expect it to be. The room and bathroom were immaculate. The bathroom was adorable, with pretty mosaic tile trim, had the best water pressure ever (standing in the shower was like standing under a waterfall), and even had a towel-warming rack. The noise in the hotel was not excessive, and we never heard the club, even though it was supposedly on the same side of the hotel as our room. The windows had both glass panes and also wooden panels that, when shut, cut out all street noise completely. We never noticed any odor around the hotel.The area was not dangerous- it's just busy, since the central market is at the end of the street. We loved wandering around it. No one ever accosted us as we left the hotel, trying to sell us watches, as one traveler stated. The merchants are in the market, not hanging around the Globus front doors. There were lots of little restaurants and shops around.The staff was wonderful, and the concierge (I think his name was Nicolas?) was friendly and accommodating. He even pulled out a map and circled places for us to check out on New Years Eve, and described exactly what festivities would be taking place at each location. The breakfast room was cozy and inviting, and the man who ran it was impeccably polite. The food and made-to-order cappucinos were excellent.We also really appreciated the free internet service- that is NOT common! No, it's not wireless, but good lord! Is it so hard to bring an ethernet cable? We paid 8 euros for one hour of internet access at another hotel! The flat-screen, satellite TV was a great perk, too. At our next hotel, an expensive 4-star place, we had an old TV which barely got 5 channels to come in.All in all, our experience at the Globus was excellent. I will continue to recommend it highly to anyone going to Florence.HeatherCharlottesville, Virginia, USA

<Author>TimHowlin
<Content>Overated! For the life of me, I do not understand why this hotel has so many good reviews on this website. We stayed her for five nights in April of the 2007. We had to prepay, which I hate doing, but I figured with all the good reviews, it was a small risk. Was I wrong. Where do I start:- Location is not that great. A pretty dodgy area, with Africans tryin to sell me drugs and fake watches the minute I walked out the door. But it is close to the train station, as is about 50 other hotels.- Noise! The hotel has no carpet, so be prepared to be awaken very early by the slamming of doors as the maids cleans rooms, and other guests come and go. And I don't mean a small noise, but a jolting, teeth rattling noise. Also the club near the hotel is still going strong, so be prepared to hear the noise from it until very early in the morning. I suppose when the AC is on, you can just close the windows, but it was not working yet for our visit.- Room is small! And we got a Superior. When I looked at the floor plan posted on the door (for fire evacuation) it looked like most of the rooms seemed to be the same size. I had a friend in a Standard room, and it seemed to be the same size as mine. So, if you MUST stay here, don't waste money on the Superior rooms.- Hotel staff was not so helpful. When I checked in, I sat my laptop on the desk. When I went to plug it in, the only two plugs reachable from the desk where being used by the TV and the minibar. When I called down to ask if they had a extension cord, I was coldly told no, and basically told to deal with it. I also asked if the had an air fan (the air movement helps me sleep) I was again told no, sorry, with no real regret from the front desk. - Starting to get a little run down. Yes, it was remodeled, but I think it must have been about the time Michangelo was finishing up on David. Time for a little titavating. An what is up with the moldy smell???- Lift. First, there is no lift to get you to the hotel lobby, which is two flights up steep stairs from street level. Then the lift from the lobby to the upper two floors is so small, and so slow, the only time you would want to use it when you have luggage. Even then, it stopped on the very LONGGGGG ride down, and I almost got stuck!Not to be too negative, there where a few things I liked about this hotel. Free internet was very nice, though it is NOT wireless in the rooms. Also the maid service was good, and they have a pretty nifty Sky satelitte entertainment system, though for the life of me, I could not figure out how to buy a pay per view movie. This stay taught me two things. Do not count on reviews posted on this website, but use them only as reference. And NEVER prepay for a hotel! We stayed two nights in the Cosmopolitan Concept Hotel which is near the airport, but only about ten minuted bus ride into town. WHAT A NICE HOTEL! And about 30 percent cheaper then this place. Please see my review that I am going to post on this website on that hotel. It was one of the nicest hotels I have ever spent the night in!

<Author>comfortnotluxury
<Content>Good location, nice hotel, great price We stayed here for 2 nights at the beginning of our stay in Tuscany. The location is a few blocks from the Santa Maria Novella train station, so it is very convenient to take the shuttle bus from the airport to the train station for Euro 4.50 and then walk to the hotel. The hotel is very close to San Lorenzo, but it is on a narrow street with very little car traffic. In fact, the street was so quiet that voices became amplified during the night, and I was awakened a couple of times by the voices of people walking by. Of course, our room fronted the street. The furnishings are very pleasant and new without being overly trendy, and the bathroom was particularly nice. Hairdryer provided. Comfortable bed. Very good breakfast, complete with meat, cheese, pate, fresh fruit (oranges, kiwis, etc while we were there), several types of bread/pastry, and of course cold cereal.When we returned to stay for one night at the end of our travels, we were informed that our room had no electricity and the electrician hadn't been able to take care of it that day. Globus had already booked us a very nice room in another hotel just a few blocks away. They gave us clear directions, and there was not a bit of fuss. Our stay at Globus had been prepaid, so we were not charged for our stay in the other hotel -- Globus covered the cost. Globus also gave us a nice apology note and a bottle of chianti classico for our troubles. It went absolutely as smoothly as you could hope, in the event of that kind of a problem. The best kind of service imaginable.

<Author>flaguy
<Content>Excellent location for touring Florence I recently spent five nights at the Globus and had an excellent stay. All of the employees I came into contact with were friendly and very helpful. The hotel is an easy walk from the train station and is situated so that you can easily walk to all the sites.I had a great rate on one of the standard doubles and had no complaints about the room. I had two twin beds pushed together to form a large king with bedside tables on each side. On the wall opposie the bed was a large wardrobe (with free electronic safe), a small desk, and TV. The bathroom was modern and the shower was a good size. There is also a towel warmer which is great for drying your hand washing. By the way, there is a coin laundry just around the corner with the instructions printed in English.The only downside was the noise level in the hotel. All of the floors are tile and the walls are a little thin but I never dug out the earplugs I always carry so it wasn't a serious problem. My window looked out onto a wing of the building so there was no street noise although there was a dance club nearby you could hear on the weekends but living in a college town, I'm used to the sounds of music in the background.If I'm ever lucky enough to make it back to Florence, I would definitely stay at the Globus.

<Content>Excellent experience We enjoyed every aspect of this hotel! Upon arrival we were greeted by a very friendly and helpful staff member. I think it is because all the floors are tile so there is a lot of echo's especially in the hallway. Like I said a pair of earplugs and you won't notice a thing.The breakfast that is served is very good, with a nice variety. There is a gentleman who runs it very well. I would recommend this hotel to anyone staying in Florence, it is a very quick walk to the train station and all attractions!

<Author>lauren_oriente
<Content>I was skeptical, but this is a really great hotel I stayed at the Hotel Globus at the end of July. Before the trip, I contacted the hotel because I read some reviews that mentioned the loud music from the dance club next door (I had booked the internet rate that does not allow you to cancel the hotel). The hotel quickly emailed me back and assured me that the dance club would be closed when I stayed there- which it was. I booked a double standard (same price as a smaller cancelable room). The room was small but what I expected for a European hotel in a big city. The room was very clean, quiet and had a view of San Lorenzo dome which was very beautiful. The air conditioning was fantastic and it felt great after a hot day of walking around in 100 degree heat! Friends that stayed in other hotels and did not have a/c. The breakfast downstairs is really great and the location is close to the train station and all the landmarks. Other reviews mentioned that they felt the area was sketchy at night but I never had a problem - yes, the streets are narrow and dark but no one ever bothered me and I was out late several nights. Because you have to climb two flights of stairs before you get to the lobby and elevator, I would not recommend this hotel to people who might have difficulty carrying their baggage up stairs. Overall, I was very pleased with the hotel and staff.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Stylish and friendly Stayed for four nights at the end of March.The major plus point of this hotel is that it is spectacular value. The rooms are spotless and stylish and the staff really friendly and welcoming. It's certainly much much better than you would expect for the price. I paid the same price for a 3 star hotel in Pisa with old, worn rooms that felt like a cell. Walking into our smart, comfortable standard room in the Globus was such a relief! The ensuite had a shower big enough for two.The building is also steps away from the Medici Chapel and San Lorenzo, and a couple of minutes from the Duomo.The downsides are what people have already mentioned- the stairs and the noise. The hotel is not accessible if you have mobility difficulties because the reception is on the first floor up a flight of stairs. Rooms on the top floor are another 2 flights up from there. This is fine if you're young and fit (and your reward for all that climbing are views of the Medici Chapel dome!), but if you're unfit and creaky like I am it's a struggle! There is a (unique) little lift, but if it's not on the right floor you'll wait ages for it to arrive.Although I agree that there is noise from the nightclub, if you close the window most of it is blocked out. I found the most noise was made by other guests. The halls and stairs are not carpeted and any noise echoes around the building. Doors slamming and luggage being hauled through the halls was a particular problem, and note that anything you say in the halls can be heard in the rooms.The final point I would make is that as a woman I did feel slightly uncomfortable with the area. There were some groups of men hanging around on the street corners so I wouldn't advise solo female travellers to stay here if they are nervous; nothing happened to me, and there are plenty of people around- but you might feel a bit intimidated. However, on the upside there's a fantastic chocolate shop right next door with more sweets than you can imagine!I have rated Globus above average because I think you'd be hard-pressed to find such a friendly hotel with such good decor and pleasant rooms for that price anywhere else in Florence (or Pisa, or Rome!).  
<Date>May 12, 2006

<Content>clean modern hotel The hotel's location near the train station was perfect. We were able to walk in 5 mintues to the train station. The hotel is within walking distance of all the major sites. Breakfast was tasty. The breakfast room was small, but the hotel itself is not very large. Internet access in the lobby area was very useful. The room is quite standard in size for a European hotel, but the bed was comfortable. There is a bar/club in the neighborhood that may wake someone up who is a light sleeper and if your window is left open. We stayed there two nights. The first night I slept right through, but the second night I woke up and heard the noise. The staff was very helpful and gave us good recomendations for dining. The hotel also made reservations for us at the Uffizi and at the Academia galleries. Reservations are a must at both of these to avoid the long lines. I emailed them a request; and shortly thereafter, I had an email back with both reservation numbers. On the whole, I would recommend this hotel to someone.

<Author>Zabadu
<Content>Hotel Globus-- A great place to stay! We recently stayed at the Hotel Globus (from April 1 to April 5) and absolutely loved it! We arrived a day earlier than scheduled, so our first nite we were in the economy double, then in the standard double after that. Yes, the economy double is a pretty cramped space, but the standard double was quite nice. The room is nice with a view of Via Sanantonino, and the bathroom is nicely equipped (although I still don't know how to use a bidet). The breakfast provided was very good, with a wide selection of breads, cheese, fruit (kiwi, oranges, apples), yoghurt, juice, NUTELLA (man I love that stuff), and excellent cappucino/tea/chocolate. The breakfast area is nicely decorated and modern.Hotel Globus' location is great. It is within walking distance to the main train station and about a ten minute walk to the main area of Florence (Duomo, Ponte Vecchio, etc). I will say that at nite it can get a little bit loud on the street down below, but it did not affect us that much.Finally, I think the biggest plus to staying at Hotel Globus is the quality of the staff that works there. Nicholas, Nick and Alessandro are an excellent source of information and were a big help to us! They really went out of their way to make sure that our stay in Florence was a good one. They gave us recommendations on cool places to eat, jazz clubs to go to, places to visit, etc. Internet access is free from noon till midnite, which is pretty huge. All in all, our stay at Hotel Globus was excellent. If you want an inexpensive (~ 110 euro/nite), very modern, clean and friendly place to stay, I'd say that you should stay at Globus. You will not be disappointed!Sorry I don't have pictures for you all right now; I will try to post another review with pictures included at a later time.

<Content>Reasonable and well located. The web site gives an idea of superior hotel but the Globus is actually a Hotel simply average.Florence is fabulous and eating in the nearby Trattoria Mario a great and unforgettable good experience.

<Author>ukjean_8
<Content>Hotel Globus, Florence, Italy March 23rd 2006 - Hotel Globus, Florence, ItalyBooked through Expedia. Thought would get a standard double room but turned out economy twin! We stood in the middle of the room and could touch each side wall with our finger tips. Needless to say it was all a bit claustrophobic. I would have said their ecomomy was more a single room for two people. The windows did not open nor the shutters. When you see the hotel video showing the rooms be aware they are not all the same. We didn't have intentions of being in our room much on a three night visit anyway but this made doubly sure of it. There was no air conditioning on to give some air either as they had heating on because the weather was still chilly. The saving grace was the shower room which although compact was newly fitted out and more than adequate if you didn't need/want to put anything down onto a surface. Toiletries included shampoo, showercap and soap. No bodylotion or shower gel. Breakfast was good as long as you didn't want brown bread, or a healthy cereal. The juice was too sweet whether grapefruit or orange. Our room was to the front of the hotel and although windows and shutters were closed there was shouting and noise until about 4 a.m. each night. (I knew this because I couldn't sleep very well in my cell and was aware of it on the hour!) I have learnt my lesson and when going to a city I will book the best room available from now on.The staff were very accommodating and helpful. All in all a central hotel well placed, everything within walking distance. Would I stay here again? If I book the best room I might it was clean and convenient with helpful staff.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great city centre location We chose this hotel because we were arriving in Florence by train and wanted somewhere that was within easy walking distance of the station. It was only five minutes and no problem to find - down a narrow little road with lots of shops and other places to stay. We had a lovely, friendly welcome and found our room to be very large (a double superior), clean and quiet, due to the double shutters and curtains - this blocked out all light and most noise and we could have easily overslept! There is a church behind the hotel and the bells start ringing at 9am though, so maybe not! We had a great view of the unmistakeably Florentine church from our window which was a nice surprise.The hotel was refurbished in 2002 and on the whole it still looks good. The breakfast was nice, as was the facility of free internet provided in the breakfast room/bar area during the day. My favourite thing about this hotel though was its handy location for the market and shops - perfect for dropping back into to whenever you need to dump all those shopping bags in your room. The bathroom had really cute 'Hotel Globus' toileteries in as well, and the minibar was pretty inexpensive compared to other places I've stayed in.Our only minor quibbles were that the double bed had a crease down the middle where it was made up from two singles stuck together, also the lift is really slow and a bit scary so we only used it to move our luggage in and out. You have to climb steps into the lobby as well so this wouldn't be a good choice of hotel for anyone who has problems with stairs.

<Author>Robbie/rocky
<Content>Well done the Globus My wife and I went to the Globus on 21/02/06 and were allocated a Double Superior Room. We found that it was not very spacious but was adequate as we didn't stay in the room for long spells. It was quite cold and we needed the additional blankets that were supplied. It was very clean and towels etc were replaced daily. The room was on the third floor and you felt like a mountain goat by the time you reached it. It was simply furnished but had the essentials that you required. The bathroom was fine and the shower was excellent. The room was situated to the rear of the building so no problems with noise other than the church bells in the early morning but what do you expect in Florence. Nothing to complain about there.The reception was fairly sparce and you wouldn't want to linger there too long. The breakfast was fine. I made do with good old corn flakes and my wife enjoyed the pastries. Don't expect bacon, eggs etcOverall the Hotel was fine and the staff as stated in other reviews could not be more helpful. Overall though, I am amazed that so many have given five stars. We would give it 3 to 4 at best. I can only think that the five star ratings are based on the attitude of the staff alone. We enjoyed our 5 day stay in Florence and if we went back we would be prepared to stay at the hotel again because the price was right. We would have been disappointed if we had paid the full rate however. If the price seems right when you book and your expectations are not too high then I don't think the Globus will disappoint. Location of the hotel for the attractions was excellent. Nothing was too far away

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great choice for any traveler I just returned from Italy les than a week ago and one of the things I keep telling my friends was how wonderful my hotel was. I went with 17 other people (school trip) and we didn't encounter a single problem. The service is excellent. The rooms are very spacious. My room had three other girls in it and we each had our own twin sized bed and plenty of room to keep our suitcases. The bathroom is large enough for two girls to get ready in. The tub/shower is large and always had hot water. Breakfast starts early (7:30) for the early birds that can't wait to see the sights and runs late (11:00)for those who enjoyed the night life the night before. The breakfast has a lot of variety including cereal which is hard to find in Italy. The staff is incredibly helpful and kind. Alessandro works the later evening shift and is very helpful in recommending excellent restaurants around town. Just ask. Everything was very clean and the maid service is excellent. We left our passports out on the desk one morning with money on accident and when we returned, they were all stacked neatly on the corner of the desk with nothing missing. It is difficult to find such amazing service. They are very inexpensive and centered in the middle of everything you want to see. They are close to the train station, the Duomo, walking distance to the Uffizi, and the Galleria dell' Accademia (Michelangelo's David). Enjoy your trip and let Hotel Globus make it even better.

<Author>runway
<Content>Cheap, clean, and helpful hotel This was a nice, very reasonablely priced hotel in Florence. It is only about a 4 block walk from the train station. The rooms were small but very clean. There was a tiny elevator that the staff used to bring up your luggage. The hotel reception is on the 2nd floor, the rooms are above that. It was a 4 or 5 block walk to main business area but only 1/2 block from the outdoor market. At night the streets were quiet but not deserted, we were never hassled. The price can't be beat, we paid 150Euros for two nights. Breakfast was ok, the staff was very helpful. If you like hanging out in your room, this is not the place to stay, the rooms are small, no lounge area in the lobby, but if you are planning to sight see all days, it is fine.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great stay at Globus Only a one night stay for us in Firenze but were really very lucky to have found Globus (thanks to everyone who bothers to add good as well as bad comments on hotels through Trip Advisor).We booked two single rooms but both had double beds in any case overlooking front of building. Both rooms had big storage units and spotless bathrooms and were cosy and warm given it was freezing outside. It was genuinely amazing to us that we'd found a hotel with such friendly multilingual staff and a clean and comfortable place to stay very close to the historic centre for the price paid. Do get yourself a good map to find the place because it's in amongst some interesting but tiny streets. It's very close to the station but don't let that put you off at all.The trattoria Palle D'Oro practically opposite was also a good place to drop in, given we'd arrived quite tired - with a good range of typical traditional favourites including steaks at very normal, not touristy prices.So congratulations to the management and staff of Hotel Globus, you've got something going that some of the higher star establishments could learn from.

<Author>georgiaguy
<Content>Perfect location, a wonderful stay The Hotel Globus is in a wonderful location. An easy 5-10 minute walk from the train station and 5-10 minutes to the Duomo area or Accademia. The street market area is just around the corner for great shopping.We had a double superior room which was the largest room we have ever had in Europe. Plenty of room to keep 2 large suitcases open and out of the way. We had a back room on the third floor with a view of the Medici Chapel. Wood floors and contemporary decor. Bath with tub/shower combo was also very large although counter and shelf space is minimal. Room kept clean and towels replaced each day. Satellite TV gets you more English language channels than just CNN for the little time you will spend in the room while in fabulous Florence.Breakfast each morning was fresh and attendant on hand for made to order coffee, tea or hot chocolate. Computer access available in breakfast room in the evenings.Staff was helpful with directions and restaurant recommendations. Several nice restaurants and tratorias within a short walk. You do have to carry bags up one flight of stairs to the first floor lobby upon arrival. From there the staff will get your bags to your room. There is a very small lift hidden away and most guests are unaware of it and use the stairs.Reasonably priced. Clean. Great location. Discount offered for advance payment with internet booking. We would definately stay at the Globus again.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>3-Star Price, 5-Star Treatment What can I say?My girlfriends and I toured all over Europe this summer, stayed at a number of three and four star hotels, but the best hotel for me is undoubtedly Globus.First of all, the location is fantastic. The Duomo is a 5-minute walk away, and so is the train station where tourists can catch the bus-tours (w/c is the best value for a quick overview of the city). We were also only a half-block away from the Mercato Centrale and street markets.Second, the room was actually pretty big compared to most European rooms we've had. We had a quad, and the room was neat, spacious and quite modern. No view, but we weren't expecting one. We even had a flat screen TV, which, given our addiction to MTV europe, was a huge plus. Third, free breakfast! Need I say more? Oh fine, we had pastries, meats, cappucinos and hot chocolate, cereal, cheeses... quite a spread really! Free internet was available in the breakfast room too.Best of all, The staff is friendly, without being obsequious. They treat you warmly, like old friends showing off their city, and hey, can even make intelligent conversation about art and history. I stayed at a 4-star in Paris, with golden-key rated conceirges, and didn't get service as good as at Globus.The staff are very friendly and helpful. Nicholas gave us great restraurant recommendations and carried our 200 lbs bags up two flights of stairs. Alessandro was very knowledgeable and helpful in recommending which museums (and museum tours) we shouldn't miss when rushing through Florence, and even helped us find train and bus schedules for our Tuscan day trips. And of course, we got made to order cappuccinos at midnight (thanks Andrea, good luck with architecture).Also, they were very patient with us, when we couldn't figure out that the AC does *NOT* work if you open windows, and when we flooded the bathroom because of shower-curtain fiascos. Oops.I miss Florence. And I love Globus. When I go back, I'll definitely stay there again.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>My favorite memories of Italy are from Globus I stayed with my three girlfriends in the Globus Hotel in Room 101 this past summer.We had been staying in four star hotels throughout our European vacation, so we thought we would be roughing it by going to a 3 star hotel. But the only rough part about this hotel was leaving it. ;-) Ha ha! No seriously, I had a great time at this hotel, but mostly because of the people I met there.I thought the staff was so great. Nicholas is very handsome, and since he was the first person we met, I knew it was going to be a good stay! ;-) Anyway, when we arrived at the hotel, he came down the stairs to greet us (they can see you coming) and he carried all of our luggage up the stairs. This was no easy feat, considering we had been shopping uncontrollably and somehow amassed a ridiculous amount of stuff. And he was very patient when I mistakenly told him that our air conditioner wasn't working and that we didn't have a phone. It turns out when you open the windows, the air conditioner doesn't work (I think we read this somewhere on this site by another reviewer, but we had forgotten). And we did have a phone, but it looked like a stapler. Anyway, Nicholas also had good recommendations for restaurants.Alessandro was so extremely helpful. (He's tall and distinguished looking, just in case you're wondering.) He gave us such good information about anything we needed: directions, schedules, information about nightlife, etc. And he also graciously helped download pictures for us so that my friend could take more on her camera. He was so accommodating, which I totally appreciated. We did cause a lot of trouble for him, unintentionally though, and actually most of that stuff really wasn't our fault! I swear! :-) When our t.v. seemed to blow out because a wire got knocked out, he came to fix it for us. And Roberto and the night-porters were cool too. Anyway, one of the guys there is very amusing. I won't mention him by name though. I thought the staff was great overall, and that's why if there were any defects in the hotel, I was able to overlook them.I agree with everyone that the location of this hotel is unbeatable. It was only a 5 minute walk from the train station and within walking distance from lots of sites. I also liked how it was close to all the stands selling leather goods. I thought the room was a good size. We had 4 twin beds in our room, so we fit comfortably. The bathroom was a decent size too. A thicker shower curtain would be good though. Breakfast was yummy. I had prunes (because I actually like them), and bread (and butter!! how I missed butter at dinner-time) and ham and fruit juices and croissants. Oh, I think housekeeping has limited hours, so you might want to consider that if you sleep in as ridiculously late as we do!While we stayed in Florence, my friend and I took the tour of the outlets which is a little outside Florence. We went to Prada, Gucci, Dolce  Gabana, etc. I think it cost us 28 euro. I think this tour was very fun. The Fendi store seemed to have lots of good deals.Anyway, one of my favorite memories from Italy does come from the Globus Hotel because that's where we heard the funniest line EVER. So this helpful guy says to us, There are three categories of people who come to Italy: those who come for the Italian food, those who come for the Italian culture, and those who come for the Italian men. If you fit in the first two categories, I can tell you where to find those things, but as for the third category, what can I say, I am here! Ha ha!

<Author>oceanlover0327
<Content>Great staff, convenient location Stayed at the Hotel Globus for three nights in September 2005. Good location, within walking distance to the train station and major sights. Also very close to the Mercato Centrale where I did most of my gift/souvenir shopping. Clean, comfortable room. I asked for a single and was pleasantly surprised to see that the room had a full sized bed instead of the usual twin sized bed. Room had a nice view of the dome of the Medici chapel which I did not expect. The staff at the Globus was the friendliest and most helpful of all the hotels I stayed at during my three week trip in Italy - especially Alessandro who always took the time to chat and offered great tips on restaurants and places to visit. Breakfast was also the best I had while in Italy - wonderful coffee, wide selection of bread, pastries, cereal, juice, cheese and jam. I highly recommend the Globus and would stay there again if I return to Florence.

<Author>hallage
<Content>Great Location What a fantastic place Florence is.....when contemplating a trip here with so many hotels it is difficult to know where to stay. I used trip advisor to rate the available hotels and we ended up at the globus hotel. The hotel is a 5 minute walk from the train station....we took a taxi not realising how close it was! The hotel is in a fantastic location right at the heart of the city right near the dome! The hotel room was small, modern but very clean and served the purpose and for the time you are actually in the room you would not need anything else. The reception staff were friendly and assisted us with dinner reservations and suggestions. At the end of the street there is a restaurant in a small square called ZA-ZA's, which is a fantastic,cheap italian which the hotel recommended and the house red wine is fantastic at 10 euros a litre. I would also recommend the restaurant at the Lungarno Hotel on the other side of the river - stunning food and location.I would go back and stay at the Globus.

<Author>Traveller075091
<Content>Good Choice We have just returned from a short stay at the Hotel Globus which we booked based on the reviews from this website. I booked the hotel over the phone as there was a problem with the website. Although I anticipated communication problems as I can't speak Italian, the man I spoke to was really nice and language was not a problem.We weren't disappointed and from the moment that we arrived at the reception desk, the staff were really friendly and cheerful. We had a standard room which was clean and nicely decorated. The breakfasts were really nice (parma ham for him and croissants and fresh bread with nutella for me) plus proper cups of tea!Easily within 5 minutes of the station concourse, we thought this hotel was really good value for money bearing in mind it was round the corner from the Duomo.In response to other reviewers: No problems with the shower (it was great - although why two heads?) or finding the hotel.If you fancy a really special meal whilst you're in Florence - Try Cibreo on Via di Macci near Santa Croce. Totally amazing (but expensive) food in their restaurant with cheaper meals in their trattoria next door.

<Author>HDM
<Content>Globus a good deal for family We stayed at the Hotel Globus for three days and liked it very much. Nick was very helpful in coming down to the street and carrying my bag up the stairs and everyone at the front desk was pleasant and helpful as well. At first, I was a little put off that we didn't get the 'view of the dome' room we had requested and when I showed Nicholas the confirming e-mail he was very apologetic and offered to move us. As we were only going to be there for three days, I declined, and he did offer us complimentary drinks in the bar. As it turns out, the room was fine. This room (101 I think) would be excellent for someone travelling with a child or teenager. Our bedroom was very large and then there was a small separate bedroom with a single bed in it which led to the large bathroom. We loved the area right near the outdoor market and the wonderful food market and everything in Florence seems to be about a five-minute walk from everything else.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great folks at the Globus As I learned from other online reviews, the folks at the 3-Star Hotel Globus in Florence are wonderful! Friendly, helpful, polite, generous with good advice for one new to the city. They willingly booked tours for museums that were not taking ticket reservations; they gave directions to help me find places I've planned to see during the day, and gave me instructions for finding particular bus stops and avoiding lines. The breakfast is a full typical European buffet--meats and cheeses, several kinds of breads, croissants, buns, cereals, two juice choices, yogurts, and best of all: coffee given with hot foamed milk in separate pitchers. There are stairs to climb to get to the hotel lobby, but that's true of many hotels in Florence, they're located on upper floors of large old buildings. There's a lift to the floors of the hotel from the lobby itself. They will hear you coming and help you carry bags up to the lobby and of course carry them down again. Fully airconditioned, mini bar and in-room safe, clean new bathrooms with bidet, TV with CNN and BBC in English. A great thing about the Globus is its location: a block from the Central Market, the San Lorenzo cathedral and market, two blocks from the train station and Santa Maria Novella church and the bus station there. A short walk to Accademia Gallery.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Nice Modern Hotel We stayed at Hotel Globus for 3 nights in May 2005. Was the only modern hotel we stayed in our trip. The front desk was very helpful. Nicholas works at night and was great. The economy rooms are very small and are two single beds pushed together. Everything was very clean and comfortable. Great breakfast and free internet from 8am until 11pm. The office is on the second floor and the elevator starts on the second floor so get ready to carry your luggage. 5 minute walk from train station. Good location in Florence. We rented a Smart car one day and drove to the outlets and Chianti. Highly suggest doing this. Was our best day in Italy. We had our laundry sent out by the hotel and was very expensive although it was in our room and folded when we arrive that night. Would definately stay at Hotel Globus again. Please remember the AC only works when you shut the window in Italy. I learned the hard way.

<Author>travelustej
<Content>Not so bad.... This is a complicated place to rate. We stayed at The Globus for two nights in May. There are some great things about the hotel. The staff is very helpful and friendly. The location is very close to the train station (easily walkable), the San Lorenzo market is a block away and everything else is easily walkable. The breakfast is also very nice and plentiful. We stayed in the economy size room which was VERY small but I knew to expect that as the hotel makes that clear. The hotel is very clean but somewhat dingy. There are minor marks on the wall and such. As far as the bathroom and sheets everything is perfectly clean. There was no smell in our room but we were told we could upgrade to a supperior for free. When we went in we immediatley noticed the smell. I am not sure that this is the fault of the hotel though. I think it just may be a sewage problem in that neighborhood of Florence. Avoid the first floor and you will be fine. I am not a small person and the bathroom in the ecomony room suited my needs fine. The walls are not thin. You can let in outdoor noise or block it out with their windows. Bottom line, it is a great value but it does have some significant problems if you are in the wrong room. Keep in mind, they are trying their best but in the end it is still a budget hotel.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>A small but cozy 3 stars hotel The hotel is on a small street (not an alley as someone reported, just a small, very old, pre-auto, cobblestone street) only about 5 minutes walk from the train station. It is in a typical old building converted to hotel use. It's up one flight of stairs and some rooms are a flight or two above. There is a one person lift from the desk area.The place is surprising modern, looking,very clean and very well kept. The desk was always staffed and the people were very professional and helpful. We stayed in the economy twin rooms and they were very small, but adequate. It was nice to have a TV with CNN and BBC to get some news. Breakfast was hands down the best we had in Italy. Fresh rolls, fruit, some dessert cake type things, ham, cereal, milk, juice, and real cappuccino Very nice man oversees it all. There is also a laptop with internet access in this room from noon on.

We also knew we would not be spending much time in the hotel.This place is a short distance from the main train station and close to the area attractions. The only issue was that the room they gave us on the first floor smelled bad. We had to open the window and leave it open all night (we were cold but at least the smell was not so bad). While they could not change us that night they did change us the next day and the new room did not smell. I would stay here if we were only going to be in the hotel 3 days max. This is mostly because I think that the hotel knows that certain rooms on the first floor are smelly, yet they still put people in the rooms. While they are willing to change you, at least they did us, given that they did not even come to inspect the room when we mentioned this issue suggests to me they are very aware of this problem. If they were to be proactive and just address this issue, then I think this place could be fine to stay in again. But given that I have noted a couple other reviews on Tripadvisor sighting this same issue, I am not confident that they will take action to solve this problem. On another note, the breakfast was good, but I was bothered that they would not let us have an option to take it or not. But for what it is worth they do provide a selection of coffee, juice, cereal, and some deli meats, so we did eat and enjoy it. Good luck.

<Content>Enjoy...!! My wife and I spent a 4 night break at hotel from 12/3/05 - 16/3/05. After getting train from Pisa Airport to the hotel we must have walked only 700 metres..the train literally picks you up from the arrivals and drops you just across the road, not far from the Globus... excellent links!! Having stayed in Italy before, we expected the rooms to be small for the rating...they were..but were ideal for what we wanted and nice and modern. Anyway, with a city as beautiful as Florence why spend any more time in your hotel than you need for (1) breakfast (2)a good nights sleep and (3) a shower before you go back out??? The staff are really friendly, good tips for local restaurants etc. but just wander yourself you can't really miss!!Biggest tip for Florence - Book all galleries and museums before you get there. It's easy to do, just call one line (--- plus country codes )and you can book all you want to see in advance because, although it was march..it is really mobbed if you don't do this.We went to the Uffizzi on the Sunday morning, picked tickets up at 9am and were inside for 9.05am..no queue, no wait but around 300 people in the non-booked queue.Superb!!!Thoroughly recommend Globus, Florence, Italy and everything within! <Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Practical, affordable, In a good Location My wife and I recently stayed at the Globus for 4 nights in March 2005. Overall we were pleased with the hotel and our stay. We booked on Expedia and had no problems with our reservations. I would have rated it higher but I had some mixed feelings on a few of the hotels features. Let me start by saying that this hotel is an excellent value for the money especially for budget minded travelers. The location is also excellent we found it convenient to just about everything in Florence. Five minute walk from the train station, about 10 to 15 to piazza della signoria and 15 to 20 minute walk to the ponte vehcio bridge. If you like to shop your right down the street from a huge open market with street vendors selling all kinds of goods and crafts. The more upscale big name designer stores are only about a 5 to 10 minute walk as well. The Hotel itself is well appointed has a modern feel thanks to contemporary furnishings in the lobby as well as in the rooms. The rooms themselves are quite small however even by Italian standards. The shower is also small but the water pressure is very good. If you have a laptop computer you have a free high speed internet connection right in your room. I found that to be one of my favorite features. The walls in this hotel are very thin and interior noise does intrude. You can hear most of the activities going on in your neighbors room or out in the hallway. If you like a lot of privacy or you may be on your honeymoon you might want to think about that. Outside or street noise is just about nonexistent thanks to two very thick glass windows. The elevator in this hotel is about the size of a small coat closet. The stairs are also very steep getting to the third floor is quite a workout especially after walking all day. I found the staff at this Hotel to be for the most part friendly and helpful. Especially Nicolas who spoke excellent English and recommended restaurants and made reservations for us. I would recommend this hotel if you are a budget minded traveler looking for comfortable, practical accommodations and have a little sense of adventure.  
<Date>Mar 22, 2005

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>I highly recommend Hotel Globus The location of Hotel Globus was great. It was right in the center of Florence and walking distance to shopping areas, restaurants and transportation. The website describes hotel as being 200 meters from the train station, which is not true. It is a bit farther. It would have been nice to know that before I carried heavy luggage to the hotel and up the stairs. You have to walk up two flights of stairs to get into the hotel. The staff was more than willing to help with the bags so this really wasn't an issue. The hotel and the common areas are very nice. There is a nice lounge area with a flat screen TV and high speed internet access. The staff is very professional and very helpful. The owner/manager, Micheal, is very good about dining suggestions, location of sights and Italian culture. The hotel was very accommodating for families with children and the rooms are very nice and newly decorated. The room temperatures were comfortable and the bathrooms were spacious and clean. The breakfast that was included was pretty good as well.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>not for a young family We stayed at the Globus in October of 2004. The hotel is near the train station but somewhat difficult to find as it is down a back alley. The sign for the hotel was not obvious either, it was merely a computer printed paper adhered to the door with tape. This should be ones first warning! The hosts were gracious but the rooms were quite musty, small, windowless and had crumbs in the bedding. Bathroom had a shower in the middle of the room with folding doors that collapsed in as you showered, subsequently soaking the room. The complimentary breakfast was adequate. The accomodations would be the equivolent of an american 2+ star hotel. Also beware for the gypsies outside, they accosted my three children outside the doors in an attempt to pickpocket my husband. Luckily we had read about such incidents and were prepared.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Loved the Hotel Globus! We spent 3 nights at the Hotel Globus this November and we had a wonderful stay. Our room was quite large for a European room and it included a Queen Bed and a separate room with a twin which would be perfect if traveling with a child.The bathroom was clean and a nice size. My only complaint would be that the shower doors were fold-away and it took some skill to keep them closed so that the bathroom floor did not get wet. Our price included breakfast every morning which included pastries, cereals, yogart, fresh fruit and cheeses. The hotel provided free internet service on a laptop in the lounge which was very convienent. We also had Satellite TV in our room which consisted of 2 english speaking channels, BBC and CNN World which is customary for Europe.The location of the hotel was great since it was a 5 minute walk to the train and it was right near the Duomo. The hotel staff was fantastic with providing us with excellent restaurants and sights to see. I would definetly return to this hotel if we visit Florence in the future.

<Content>Honeymoon in Globus We had the first week of our honeymoon at the Globus Hotel. Stayed in a Superior Double which was large and spacious. At the weekends it was a little noisy at night (from about 11pm) due to the nightclub that backed onto the hotel...but we were really too tired from the walking for this to be a real problem.Would have no trouble recommending this hotel.

<Author>LCovert
<Content>Felt Like Home We enjoyed our stay at the Hotel Globus. The best aspect of this hotel is the people and the service provided. They were warm, friendly and helpful and made us feel at home. It was great coming back to the hotel, coming home, after a long day of site-seeing to be greeted with smiles. The hotel has an updated contemporary feel with small rooms that are sufficient but not special.The hotel is located just blocks from the train station which is great. Pulling luggage to the hotel was not without a bit of a struggle given the uneven pavement and significant traffic. There is much to offer around the hotel (restaurants, stores, market) but with the exception of some of the restaurants, much closes after 6.The lounge offers a nice breakfast in the morning, convenient internet service and a place to gather with friends or family.I recommend staying at the Hotel Globus if you want a reasonably priced, no frills hotel with great service in a convenient tourist location.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Hotel Globus is wonderful Of all the places we stayed on our vacation in Italy, Hotel Globus was our favorite. The english speaking hotel staff was very helpful, made us feel welcome, and gave us a map of the city upon arrival. For the money, this is a great hotel, and we would all recommend it to anyone traveling to Florence.

<Author>Waipahu
<Content>Great value and staff, but avoid room 101 Stayed at Globus July 18-21 based on tripadvisor reviews, and was extremely pleased with the value. My only complaint would be to avoid room 102 - there was a faint sewage odor, which explained why an automatic air freshener was in the room. It didn't always mask the odor, and was quite loud when it went off. Also, 101 is near a door that leads to the breakfast room and common computer, which resulted in frequent door slamming and loud conversation that could be heard in the room. Maybe a better insulated room door would help this problem. I would have asked to change rooms, but the hotel was completely booked. To clarify a comment by a recent reviewer - there is no elevator from street level to the reception desk, which is one floor above street level, but there IS a tiny elevator from the reception area to the upper floor rooms. When I arrived and rang the bell, someone came down to help me take my bag up the stairs. Globus has a great staff!

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Hotel Globus--Outstanding The Hotel Globus is truly a gem, and a part of me wants to keep it secret from the traveling hordes. Obviously this hotel owner has taste, and appreciates good design---the modern yet comfortable interior (tastefully decorated with understated flair, Jacob Jensen phones, sleek and solid furniture, personal safe), small but functional and very clean bathroom (all rooms have showers only, I'm told), and sharply dressed staff. The breakfast was great, the coffee outstanding---not an extensive selection, but made up for by the quality of each item, from the ham to the selection of fresh fruits and yogurt. Each room has TV internet access, and there's also a PC you can use in the small but impeccably furnished interior. One look at the Globus webpage and brochure, and you know the owner/manager is trend savvy and insists on good design. The little things added up to a great stay, but best of all, what a staff---young and courteous, and friendly in a comfortable way without being superficially chummy (if you've traveled through the US midwest, you probably know what I mean). Just minutes from the train station and the city center, too. Best hotel in Florence for the price, no doubt.  
<Date>Jul 14, 2004

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Loved the globus and the neighborhood! We booked The Globus based on reviews we read here and were so pleased. Great location; we took the city bus from the airport to the train station, then pulled our luggage to the hotel from there! We were on the third floor on the back with great view of the Medici Chapel dome and bell tower over the tops of nearby flats, which had laundry hanging on clotheslines out their windows...perfect! We were there in mid June and the nights were cool. The room was air conditioned, but we kept our fabulous big windows flung open to enjoy the night air and woke to the pealing bells and cooing pidgeons on the roof next door. Just up the street was the city market with outdoor dining in the square until quite late. We loved it! A very pleasant breakfast was served each morning by an equally pleasant gentleman. Small hotel, but well appointed with quality furnishings and grand windows.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great value!! We spent 4 nights at Hotel Globus and thought it was an excellent value for the money. We had chosen it based on these reviews and it did not disappoint. We had a superior double room. It was a very good sized room and the modern decor was cool. The AC went full blast and the bathroom was a good size for a European hotel. The room was very clean and they gave us fresh towels every day. The people were very friendly and helpful - we especially thought the man who set up breakfast was very accomodating with the made to order caffes. Breakfast had a nice variety with fresh fruit, pastries, yogurt, cereal, etc. The hotel is in a very convenient location - only a five-minute walk to the Duomo and a two-minute walk to the train station. I wouldn't hang out there really late at night or anything but I felt very safe at the hotel. And yes, to get to the reception requires climbing a flight of stairs, but really no different then carrying my luggage up the stairs at home. All in all, I thought we lucked out with the Globus and we would definitely recommend it to other visitors to Florence!

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Excellent hotel with a warm, professional and friendly staff When I booked our various Italian lodgings, it was with great trepidation since we had never been to Europe. Reading guide books and hearing the experiences of a friend who had been in Italy recently were our only preparation. Arriving at the Globus dispelled all fears. From that moment forward, every member of the staff bent over backwards to welcome us warmly, answer any question, offer advice, make arrangements or recommendations or help a guest with anything whatsoever that he or she might need. The rooms were clean, modern and completely comfortable. There was never a shortage of hot water or clean towels. A laptop computer in the breakfast room was available to guests most of the day and into the evening. The breakfasts equalled or surpassed those at our other Italian lodgings. Our superior double room had a balcony with a grand view of the Basilica di San Lorenzo cupola and Medici Chapel rooftops. The location is exceptionally convenient to the San Lorenzo markets, Santa Maria Novella church and the rail/bus stations. Of course, in Florence, all the hot spots are in a relatively small area. If, like me, you want more than the very modest mom and pop pensione but not the price or luxuries of a 5-star hotel, book the Globus with confidence.  
<Date>Apr 16, 2004

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Clean, modern and central but small - good shower and comfortable beds! Very clean and recently decorated but the room was very small. Our economic twin room was very narrow (only just wider than 2 small single beds)and the bathroom was very cramped with no where to put your toiletries (no shelves or vanity cabinet - just a free standing basin). The reception area and staff were all very good and quite helpful. The breakfast area was modern and clean and a nice breakfast (ceral, fruit, bread and croissants, juice and hot drinks) was avaialbe from 7:30am. The location was good if you like to be central and don't mind a bit of noise (recommend ear plugs for a good nights sleep). The Duomo is just 3 mins walk away and the other sites are all within 10 mins walk. For those with a car I recommend you park outside the restricted area. Parking on Viale Spartaco Lavagnini is free from 8pm till 8am not like the garages that will charge 24 euro a night. I would stay at Hotel Globus again - but next time in a larger room :o)

<Content>an excellent 3 stars hotel I would highly recommend the Globus. Of all the hotels I stayed in on my trip to Italy, this was by far the best.
