<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Modern-minimalis design and Clean We booked a reservation at the Hotel Globus through its web-site based of the good reviews that we read on tripadvisor. Though, we are fully aware that european hotels are less in quality compared with the ones in Asia or US. This is true, therefore we are not expecting much on it.During the time to confirm our reservation, we have been offered with various rate for double standard or double executive room. Thank you to Michelle who is one of the owner of this hotel. He gave us a good deal of Euro 90 for double executive room (incl. buffet breakfast and taxes). We stayed there for 3 nights late December 2003.To us the hotel is most likely a 2 stars with a 4 stars bathroom facility. Our room is spacious with internet access, cozy modern-minimalis design and clean. The one which decreased the value of this hotel is that the lobby is up a flight of stairs. Guests must climb with luggage. when we arrived we were greeted by the front staff who helped us to bring our luggages up to the lobby.We left our luggages at the front desk since the room reserved for us was still occupied. When we came back in the afternoon, our luggages had been brought in the room at 2nd floor. The bar and breakfast place looked like a snack vendor and the only staff is very practical. Breakfast was fine european standard with fresh fruit, however we could ask for a cup of capucinno or even a glass of hot chocolate.This hotel is recommended for budget travelers who do not mind to carry on your own luggages to the room and during check out. We do not mind it either. The location is best, near the train station (5 minutes walk) and many budget eating houses nearby. Mercato St. Lorenzo is just steps from the hotel. The window of our room is facing the back of Medici Chapel, a warm scene in the morning of winter season.We will absolutely stay there again if we get back to Florence one day.xxx

<Author>amarillo
<Content>Central with 'chic' decoration I stayed for 3 nights in October 2003 - very central, just a few minutes walk from all the main tourist sites of Florence and a 10 minute walk from the railway station ( although the website map could be a little clearer - I know Florence well and I got lost getting to the hotel from the station ).A double flight of stairs from the street is a drawback, but you could wait at the bottom and wave to the Reception staff via the security camera to get them to carry your luggage up, I suppose. <Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Dary, Dingy, and Cheap I booked a reservation at the Hotel Globus in Florence based of the good reviews that I read on Trip advisor and the hotel website. Boy was I mislead! This hotel is no more than a one star hotel. I have stayed in Holiday Inns that are nicer than this. The room might be cheap. Mine was 170 euros but you definitely get what you pay for. The room was pretty clean but the hotel was dark and deserted. I arrived and found that the lobby was up a flight of stairs which I had to climb by myself with all my luggage at midnight and once I got the the room that they were calling lobby I had to yell hello before the one person who was on staff at the hotel came out. The bar and breakfast place looked like a fraternity house and the staff was rude. Needless to say I stayed on night and then checked into the Hotel Lungarno and had a fantastic stay there. Don't believe the other reviews! This place is a DUMP!

<Author>dogstar88
<Content>Good Value We reserved a small twin room after reading reviews here and Expedia. The room was small but this is what we expected and did not spend much time in the room anyway. Our room was 206 overlooking the Via San. Antonino and the windows were great, quite soundproof keeping out the extensive street noise when we desired. We actually liked having it open during the day listening to the sounds of the market and the street.The location was great. It wasn't in the midst of the touristic chaos and was easy walking distance from the Duomo, Accademia, Uffizi and expecially the train station.My favorite part of this place was the service. Allesandro made just great restaurant recommendations and was even willing to help us with our train reservations....even though he was swamped with other stuff. He never missed on the restaurants....someone commented to me that they probably get a kickback on the recommendations....WHO CARES...it was great food and didn't cost us anything extra.Great value and location....not the lap of luxury but perfect for the common sense traveler who isn't fluent in Italian.

<Author>bevchris
<Content>Great Hotel and fantastic location We spent 8 night at the Hotel Globus and loved it. The staff were very friendly and helpful. Our room had a small balcony whist was nice. The room was spacious on european standards. The breakfasts were good too. The location could not be better, just a short stroll at most main sights, eg Duomo etc. The corridor noise was a little noisy due to the tiled floor but soundproofing between rooms was very good. We would definately stay here again without hesitation.
